					<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  // Select all stop buttons across the page
  const stopButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.myButton_stop');

  stopButtons.forEach(stopBtn => {
    const parent = stopBtn.closest('.playcard');

    // Use MutationObserver to watch style changes
    const observer = new MutationObserver(mutations => {
      mutations.forEach(mutation => {
        if (mutation.type === 'attributes' && mutation.attributeName === 'style') {
          const display = stopBtn.style.display;

          if (display === 'inline') {
            parent.classList.add('playing');
          } else {
            parent.classList.remove('playing');
          }
        }
      });
    });

    observer.observe(stopBtn, {
      attributes: true,
      attributeFilter: ['style']
    });
  });
});
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        soundManager.useFlashBlock = true; // optional - if used, required flashblock.css
        soundManager.url = 'https://lycaradio.com/wp-content/plugins/compact-wp-audio-player/swf/soundmanager2.swf';
        function play_mp3(flg, ids, mp3url, volume, loops)
        {
            //Check the file URL parameter value
            var pieces = mp3url.split("|");
            if (pieces.length > 1) {//We have got an .ogg file too
                mp3file = pieces[0];
                oggfile = pieces[1];
                //set the file URL to be an array with the mp3 and ogg file
                mp3url = new Array(mp3file, oggfile);
            }

            soundManager.createSound({
                id: 'btnplay_' + ids,
                volume: volume,
                url: mp3url
            });

            if (flg == 'play') {
    stop_all_tracks();                soundManager.play('btnplay_' + ids, {
                    onfinish: function() {
                        if (loops == 'true') {
                            loopSound('btnplay_' + ids);
                        }
                        else {
                            document.getElementById('btnplay_' + ids).style.display = 'inline';
                            document.getElementById('btnstop_' + ids).style.display = 'none';
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
            else if (flg == 'stop') {
    //soundManager.stop('btnplay_'+ids);
                soundManager.pause('btnplay_' + ids);
            }
        }
        function show_hide(flag, ids)
        {
            if (flag == 'play') {
                document.getElementById('btnplay_' + ids).style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('btnstop_' + ids).style.display = 'inline';
            }
            else if (flag == 'stop') {
                document.getElementById('btnplay_' + ids).style.display = 'inline';
                document.getElementById('btnstop_' + ids).style.display = 'none';
            }
        }
        function loopSound(soundID)
        {
            window.setTimeout(function() {
                soundManager.play(soundID, {onfinish: function() {
                        loopSound(soundID);
                    }});
            }, 1);
        }
        function stop_all_tracks()
        {
            soundManager.stopAll();
            var inputs = document.getElementsByTagName("input");
            for (var i = 0; i < inputs.length; i++) {
                if (inputs[i].id.indexOf("btnplay_") == 0) {
                    inputs[i].style.display = 'inline';//Toggle the play button
                }
                if (inputs[i].id.indexOf("btnstop_") == 0) {
                    inputs[i].style.display = 'none';//Hide the stop button
                }
            }
        }
    </script>

      (function () {
        // console.log($1);

        function createPlayer(item) {
  if (!item || !item.storage_file_url || !item.name) return "";

  const title = item.name || "Untitled Recording";
  const image = item.artwork?.thumbnail_path || item.artwork?.path || "";
  const description = item.description || "";
  const playerId = `audio_${item.uuid}`;
  /*const createdDate = item.created_at 
    ? new Date(item.created_at).toLocaleDateString('en-GB', { day: '2-digit', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' }) 
    : "Unknown";*/
  const createdDate = item.created_at 
  ? new Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-GB', {
      weekday: 'short',
      day: '2-digit',
      month: 'short',
      year: 'numeric',
      timeZone: 'Europe/London'
    }).format(new Date(item.created_at)) 
  : "Unknown";

  if (!window.timbrePlayers) window.timbrePlayers = [];
  window.timbrePlayers.push(playerId);

  return `
    <div class='playlist-item' data-id='${playerId}' data-src='${item.storage_file_url}' data-title='${title}' data-image='${image}' data-description='${description}'>
      ${image ? `<img src='${image}' alt='Artwork'>` : ''}
      <div style='flex:1;'>
        <div style='font-weight:500;'>${title}</div><div style='font-size:0.85rem;color:#666;'>${createdDate}</div>
        <div class='now-playing-label' style='font-size:0.85rem;color:#08DC7D;display:none;'>Playing</div>
      </div>
      <div class='playicon'><img src="https://lycaradio.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/05/blue_play.svg" alt="Play" class="play"> <img src="https://lycaradio.com/wp-content/uploads/2025/05/green_stop.svg" alt="Play" class="pause">
      </div>
    </div>`;
}

        function bindSeekbars() {
          document.querySelectorAll("audio").forEach(audio => {
            const seek = document.getElementById("seek_" + audio.id);
            if (!seek) return;
            audio.addEventListener("timeupdate", () => {
              if (!isNaN(audio.duration)) {
                seek.max = audio.duration;
                seek.value = audio.currentTime;
              }
            });
            seek.addEventListener("input", () => {
              audio.currentTime = seek.value;
            });
          });
        }

        function loadRecordingsForDate(dateText) {
  const wrapper = document.querySelector(".timbre-recordings-wrapper");
  if (!wrapper) return;

  const customer = wrapper.dataset.customer;
  const feed = wrapper.dataset.feed;
  const results = wrapper.querySelector(".timbre-recordings-results");
  results.innerHTML = "<div style='padding:1rem;text-align:center;'>Loading recordings...</div>";

  // Format the selected date into the required API format
  const date = new Date(dateText);
  const formattedDate = date.toISOString().split('T')[0];  // Format as YYYY-MM-DD

  // Create the filter query for the API (using the start and end time of the selected date)
  const startDate = `${formattedDate} 00:00:00`;  // Start of the day
  const endDate = `${formattedDate} 23:59:59`;    // End of the day

  const filters = `created_at:gt:${startDate},created_at:lt:${endDate},published:eq:1,type:eq:1`;

  jQuery.ajax({
    url: "https://lycaradio.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php",
    method: "POST",
    dataType: "json",
    data: {
      action: "fetch_timbre_recordings",
      nonce: "7447b02733",
      customer,
      feed,
      limit: 0,
      filters: filters // Send the filters as part of the API request
    },
    success: function (response) {
      if (!response.success || !Array.isArray(response.data?.data)) {
        results.innerHTML = "<div>No recordings found or API error.</div>";
        return;
      }

      const filtered = response.data.data.filter(item => {
        if (!item.created_at) return false;
        const itemDateStr = item.created_at.split('T')[0];
        return itemDateStr === formattedDate;
      });

      const sorted = filtered.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.created_at) - new Date(a.created_at));
      const first = sorted[0];
      const html = sorted.map(createPlayer).join('');
      results.innerHTML = `
        <div class='main-player-area'>
          <div class='player-bg' id='player-bg' style="background-image:url('${first.artwork?.thumbnail_path || first.artwork?.path || ''}');">
            <div class='overlay' style='position:absolute;inset:0;background:linear-gradient(to top, rgba(0,0,0,0.7), transparent);z-index:1;'></div>
            <div class='player-ui' style='position:relative;z-index:2;padding:1rem;'>
              <div id='player-date' style='font-size:0.85rem;color:#ccc;margin-bottom:0.5rem;'>${new Date(first.created_at).toLocaleDateString('en-GB', { day: '2-digit', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' }).replace(/ /g, ' ')}</div>
              <div id='player-title' style='font-weight:bold;color:#fff;font-size:1.2rem;'>${first.name || ''}</div>
              <marquee id='player-description' style='font-size:0.9rem;color:#ccc;'>${first.description || ''}</marquee>
              <audio id='main-player' controls src='${first.storage_file_url}' style='width:100%;margin-top:0.5rem;background:#000;border-radius:6px;padding:0.5rem;'></audio>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div class='playlist-container'>${html}</div>`;
      
      document.querySelectorAll('.playlist-item').forEach(item => {
        item.addEventListener('click', () => {
          const audio = document.getElementById('main-player');
          const title = document.getElementById('player-title');
          const img = document.getElementById('player-image');
          const desc = document.getElementById('player-description');

          document.querySelectorAll('.playlist-item').forEach(i => {
            i.classList.remove('active');
            const label = i.querySelector('.now-playing-label');
            if (label) label.style.display = 'none';
          });
          item.classList.add('active');
          const label = item.querySelector('.now-playing-label');
          if (label) label.style.display = 'block';
          const toggle = document.querySelector('.play-toggle');
          if (toggle) toggle.textContent = '⏸';
          audio.src = item.dataset.src;
          title.textContent = item.dataset.title;
          if (item.dataset.image) {
            document.getElementById('player-bg').style.backgroundImage = `url('${item.dataset.image}')`;
          }
          desc.textContent = item.dataset.description;
          audio.play();
        });
      });
    },
    error: function (xhr, status, error) {
      console.error("❌ AJAX error:", error);
      results.innerHTML = "<p>Failed to load recordings.</p>";
    }
  });
}


        function initTimbre() {
          const picker = document.getElementById("timbre-date-picker");
          if (!picker || typeof jQuery === "undefined") {
            console.warn("⛔ Datepicker not available. Retrying...");
            return setTimeout(initTimbre, 500);
          }

          const today = new Date();
          const yyyy = today.getFullYear();
          const mm = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
          const dd = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
          const todayStr = `${yyyy}-${mm}-${dd}`;
          picker.value = todayStr;

          jQuery(picker).datepicker({
            dateFormat: "yy-mm-dd",
            defaultDate: todayStr,
            changeMonth: true,
            changeYear: true,
            showOtherMonths: true,
            maxDate: 0,
            /*onSelect: function (dateText) {
              loadRecordingsForDate(dateText);
            }*/
            onSelect: function (dateText) {
                // Format the date as dd MM yy for user-friendly display
                var formattedDate = jQuery.datepicker.formatDate('dd MM yy', new Date(dateText));

                // Update the input field with the formatted date
                picker.value = formattedDate;

                // Load recordings based on the selected date (use yyyy-mm-dd format)
                loadRecordingsForDate(dateText);
            },
            beforeShowDay: function(date) {
            // This ensures the selected date gets highlighted
              var selectedDate = new Date(picker.value);
              // Check if the current date being processed matches the selected date
              if (selectedDate && date.getTime() === selectedDate.getTime()) {
              // Return an array: [selectable, CSS_class, tooltip]
                return [true, 'highlight-selected-date', 'Selected Date'];
              } else {
                return [true, '', '']; // Default for other dates
              }
            }
            /*,
            beforeShowDay: function(date) {
            // This ensures the selected date gets highlighted
              var selectedDate = new Date(picker.value);
              return [true, (date.getDate() === selectedDate.getDate() &&
                date.getMonth() === selectedDate.getMonth() &&
                date.getFullYear() === selectedDate.getFullYear()) ? 'ui-state-active' : ''];
            }*/
          });
          /*jQuery(picker).datepicker("setDate", todayStr);*/
          loadRecordingsForDate(todayStr);
        }

        window.addEventListener("load", initTimbre);
      })();
    </script>
        <script>
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
        // Delay slightly to ensure other DOMContentLoaded scripts have run
        setTimeout(function () {
            const wpCurrentTime = "11:01";
            const wpCurrentDay = "tuesday"; // lowercase to match data-day

            function timeToMinutes(timeStr) {
                const [hours, minutes] = timeStr.split(':').map(Number);
                return hours * 60 + minutes;
            }

            const currentMinutes = timeToMinutes(wpCurrentTime);

            const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.schedule-card-2');
            cards.forEach(card => {
                const cardDay = card.getAttribute('data-day'); // e.g. "monday"
                const start = card.getAttribute('data-start-time');
                const end = card.getAttribute('data-end-time');

                if (!cardDay || !start || !end) return;

                const startMinutes = timeToMinutes(start);
                const endMinutes = timeToMinutes(end);

                const isToday = wpCurrentDay === cardDay;
                const isNow = currentMinutes >= startMinutes && currentMinutes <= endMinutes;

                if (isToday && isNow) {
                    card.classList.add('now-playing');
                }
            });
        }, 100); // slight delay (100ms) to ensure previous script finishes
    });
    </script>

				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );
			</script>
